14b5(12): / sangs rgyas par thog/ lung rtogs bstan pa'i rnying po gang / sring pa'i mthar yang gnas pa dang / res med bstan 'dzin sgkyes bu'i tshogs/ 'gro dan gegs med lhun grub thog/ yangs pa'i zhing 
14b6(12): khams thams cad du / nad mtshon lu gae rgyun chad nas/ 'gro rnams zhi bde' dpal yen la/ longs su spyod pa'i bkra nyis thog/ ces pa'i 'bel dtsem chen cmig 'di nyid gsung dung ben gyi gnas 
15a1(12): / by/ dpal ldan bri btan nod bi'i dbe nas tlob dpen gyi ling 'dzin changs pa bstan 'dzin 'og pas r#ragrnyen bris te phral bo// khus bgregs chan pa'i gsal bsh// sgang gsal ngan / 
15a2(12): / sang rge gcod kyi moed dang / gang gsal ngan song g gocod kyi mod ye ma dpe byung p cha yan nag chang nam rgyal g.yang dag can gnod bzhag theg dbal bka' bcas dp gyun mi 'dra ba 'ga' la 'dra bslud byas se// dge 
15a3(12): syed yan lag gsum pa dang / gsung dung ljang bshags kyi lod chag dang / gsung du sems dpa'i lung ba bshags pa'i mo// ngansong dang srug/ sdeg bshags gsed gyi sra gri/ mna' bshags den cen 'phreng ba'i brul lod / 
15a4(12): bcas kyi ma ds ni// bal bhyung dgen pa'i bka' 'gyur 'phrul dpar can gyi gras su yed pa gzhod bnag theg// pe rgyun ma 'dra ba 'ga' dang 'dra bsdud byas/ dgo myed yan lag gsum pa ni/ byung po go nad stdag tsha / 
15a5(12): bzed pa don ldan gyi lag bres yig nag dp nying can la 'dra bsnud byas/ phyogs btsu' mun sel gyi ma dp ni/ byung s thams nyin rkang chung chang gi gzungs 'das lag bhres yig nag dpo ning can nad dang / gnam / 
15a6(12): sa snang brgyad kyi ma dpe ni/ byung po gsed tsha zhu blua bstan 'dzin grags pa'i lag bris yig nag gzungs 'das nad dang / sa bgdag bshags 'bum gyi ma dp ni/ byung po go snad rgom pa tshang gi lag bris yig nag can / 
15b1(12): ndad gznod bzhag byas nas bgrigs yo// gong 'ag gi mla ds chag la bris pa'i chad lhag dang mngon gsal can gyi rkyen ma then rdegs la cha brkangs byas pa las gang byung gis bcos thal ma byas par// ni bzhi mdzod / 
15b2(12): lnga'i dp rning phyogs bgrigs / kyo a grangs paspad zhus bgrigs byas yed kyang ddaung ma rtegs dbang gis ca lhagsegs yod nges te/ spyi la rbyad sngen lo nga lnga brgya ldag nas gangs can nad kyi yul / 
15b3(12): du yi go' par chang 'jzugs bskun dang // se gzhi legs bgrigs byas pa'i 'grems syel yengs khyab byed srel dad zen na'ang / g.yung dung ban gyi dpe gzhi' bsdu bgrigs byed pa'o ga skabs kyi thed yug de tsal byung med / 
15b4(12): pas/ 'did phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig zhes len gni dken pas gom cha gsad du yin pa dang / ghes su de zhus bgrigs pa tche yang mkhyen dbyed rab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di' thad mthun / 
15b5(12): rkyen rung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig p dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang so'i ched yug dang gnas sdangs tsha las brgal ba'i legs ma zhig then thabs med pas// e lcugs kyis rjes su gzigs /
